	if (!is_file('includes/classes/http_class.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/http_class.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/http_class.class.php') != 'aa54edbe8515768795ce36586eeae2fb66111f7f') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/http_class.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/http_class.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/http_class.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/http_class.class.php') !== 'aa54edbe8515768795ce36586eeae2fb66111f7f') {

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/http_class.class.php');

			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/http_class.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/http_class.class.php') !== 'aa54edbe8515768795ce36586eeae2fb66111f7f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/http_class.class.php');

	if (!is_file('includes/vnag_framework.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/vnag_framework.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/vnag_framework.inc.php') != '49fbde706a5bcae4c80a1396f332c62dc8396471') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/vnag_framework.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/vnag_framework.inc.php', 0644)) {

	}

	if (@sha1_file('includes/vnag_framework.inc.php') !== '49fbde706a5bcae4c80a1396f332c62dc8396471') {

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/vnag_framework.inc.php');

			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/vnag_framework.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/vnag_framework.inc.php') !== '49fbde706a5bcae4c80a1396f332c62dc8396471') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/vnag_framework.inc.php');

	writefile_10();
	if (!is_file('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php') != '7f157f7abe8650aeec272a620107ef4c893a0b55') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php') !== '7f157f7abe8650aeec272a620107ef4c893a0b55') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php') !== '9b91f5b05dfee483b944f4ec416e29963905f71f') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php') !== '7f157f7abe8650aeec272a620107ef4c893a0b55') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
		}
	}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php') != 'd4f5c686e0f965e3ac018d29281bdb25542e7176') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php');
	}

	if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php') !== 'd4f5c686e0f965e3ac018d29281bdb25542e7176') {

			if (!@copy('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_12();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php') !== 'd4f5c686e0f965e3ac018d29281bdb25542e7176') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php');

	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/database/pgsql/plugin.inc.php') != '02acedc5f606bf5c5684860d3b6fdd2deef7e42c') {

	}

if (!is_file('plugins/database/sqlite3/plugin.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/database/sqlite3/plugin.inc.php');
	writefile_14();
	if (!is_file('plugins/database/sqlite3/plugin.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/database/sqlite3/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/database/sqlite3/plugin.inc.php') != 'af4bfa1474c8ccb7e6e717eff1563d1e65b6a4a3') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/sqlite3/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database/sqlite3/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/database/sqlite3/plugin.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/sqlite3/plugin.inc.php') !== 'af4bfa1474c8ccb7e6e717eff1563d1e65b6a4a3') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/sqlite3/plugin.inc.php') !== '672869e327ccb1058136e0b4779b91a113dce14d') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/database/sqlite3/plugin.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/database/sqlite3/plugin.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/database/sqlite3/plugin.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/database/sqlite3/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_14();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/sqlite3/plugin.inc.php') !== 'af4bfa1474c8ccb7e6e717eff1563d1e65b6a4a3') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/sqlite3/plugin.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	writefile_15();
	if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') != 'f0ccc0dbc00a6137c3f868ce8d672310b7fe24c2') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== 'f0ccc0dbc00a6137c3f868ce8d672310b7fe24c2') {
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== 'ceda92f0f92b42f444b1a402224ffde1e095d247') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_15();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== 'f0ccc0dbc00a6137c3f868ce8d672310b7fe24c2') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
		}
	}
